Introduction\n\n### 1.1 What is iTechSmart Supreme?\n\niTechSmart Supreme is an **autonomous IT infrastructure healing platform** that:\n- **Detects** issues in real-time across your infrastructure\n- **Diagnoses** root causes using AI-powered analysis\n- **Resolves** problems automatically with secure command execution\n- **Notifies** your team through multiple channels\n- **Logs** everything for compliance and audit\n\n### 1.2 Key Benefits\n\nâœ… **Reduce Downtime** - Resolve issues in seconds, not hours  \nâœ… **Save Time** - Automate repetitive troubleshooting tasks  \nâœ… **Improve Security** - Rapid response to security threats  \nâœ… **Ensure Compliance** - Complete audit trail of all actions  \nâœ… **Scale Operations** - Manage thousands of servers effortlessly  \n\n### 1.3 Who Should Use This Manual?\n\n- **IT Operations Teams** - Day-to-day monitoring and management\n- **System Administrators** - Configuration and deployment\n- **DevOps Engineers** - Integration and automation\n- **Security Teams** - Security monitoring and incident response\n- **IT Managers** - Oversight and reporting\n\n---\n\n## 2. Getting Started\n\n### 2.1 System Requirements\n\n**Minimum Requirements:**\n- CPU: 2 cores\n- RAM: 4GB\n- Disk: 20GB\n- OS: Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+, CentOS 8+, Debian 11+)\n\n**Recommended for Production:**\n- CPU: 4+ cores\n- RAM: 8GB+\n- Disk: 50GB+ SSD\n- Network: 1Gbps\n\n### 2.2 Installation Methods\n\n#### Option A: Docker (Recommended)\n\n```bash\n# 1. Clone repository\ngit clone https://github.com/yourusername/itechsmart-supreme.git\ncd itechsmart-supreme\n\n# 2. Configure environment\ncp .env.example .env\nnano .env\n\n# 3. Start application\ndocker-compose up -d\n\n# 4. Verify installation\ndocker-compose ps\ndocker-compose logs -f\n```\n\n#### Option B: Manual Installation\n\n```bash\n# 1. Install Python 3.11+\nsudo apt update\nsudo apt install python3.11 python3-pip\n\n# 2. Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n\n# 3. Configure environment\ncp .env.example .env\nnano .env\n\n# 4. Run application\npython main.py\n```\n\n### 2.3 First-Time Setup\n\n1. **Access Dashboard**: Open `http://localhost:5000` in your browser\n2. **Set Master Password**: Create a strong master password for credential encryption\n3. **Add First Host**: Add your first monitored server\n4. **Configure Monitoring**: Connect to Prometheus/Wazuh\n5. **Test Alert**: Trigger a test alert to verify setup\n\n### 2.4 Quick Verification\n\n```bash\n# Check health\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/health\n\n# Expected response:\n{\n  "status": "healthy",\n  "version": "1.0.0",\n  "uptime": 3600\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Dashboard Guide\n\n### 3.1 Dashboard Overview\n\nThe iTechSmart Supreme dashboard provides real-time visibility into your infrastructure:\n\n**Main Sections:**\n1. **System Status** - Overall health indicator\n2. **Active Alerts** - Current issues requiring attention\n3. **Recent Actions** - Latest remediation actions\n4. **Pending Approvals** - Actions awaiting approval\n5. **Audit Log** - Complete action history\n\n### 3.2 Dashboard Features\n\n#### Real-Time Updates\n- **WebSocket Connection** - Live updates without page refresh\n- **Auto-Refresh** - Configurable refresh intervals\n- **Status Indicators** - Color-coded health status\n\n#### Alert Cards\nEach alert displays:\n- **Severity** - Critical, High, Medium, Low\n- **Source** - Prometheus, Wazuh, GitHub, etc.\n- **Host** - Affected server/service\n- **Message** - Alert description\n- **Timestamp** - When detected\n- **Actions** - Available remediation options\n\n#### Action Buttons\n- **Approve** - Approve pending action\n- **Reject** - Reject proposed action\n- **View Details** - See full alert information\n- **Manual Action** - Execute custom command\n\n### 3.3 Navigation\n\n**Top Menu:**\n- **Dashboard** - Main overview\n- **Alerts** - Alert management\n- **Actions** - Action history\n- **Hosts** - Managed servers\n- **Settings** - Configuration\n- **Logs** - Audit logs\n\n**Quick Actions:**\n- **Kill Switch** - Emergency stop button\n- **Refresh** - Manual refresh\n- **Filter** - Filter by severity/source\n- **Search** - Search alerts/actions\n\n### 3.4 Status Indicators\n\n| Color | Status | Meaning |\n|-------|--------|---------|\n| ðŸŸ¢ Green | Healthy | All systems operational |\n| ðŸŸ¡ Yellow | Warning | Minor issues detected |\n| ðŸŸ  Orange | Degraded | Performance issues |\n| ðŸ”´ Red | Critical | Immediate attention required |\n| âš« Gray | Unknown | No data available |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Monitoring Configuration\n\n### 4.1 Prometheus Integration\n\n#### Setup Steps\n\n1. **Configure Prometheus Endpoint**\n```bash\n# In .env file\nPROMETHEUS_ENDPOINTS=http://prometheus:9090\n```\n\n2. **Add Prometheus Alerts**\n```yaml\n# prometheus.yml\nalerting:\n  alertmanagers:\n    - static_configs:\n        - targets: [\'itechsmart:5000\']\n```\n\n3. **Configure Alert Rules**\n```yaml\n# alert_rules.yml\ngroups:\n  - name: itechsmart\n    rules:\n      - alert: HighCPU\n        expr: cpu_usage > 80\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: "High CPU on {{ $labels.instance }}"\n```\n\n#### Monitored Metrics\n\n- **CPU Usage** - Processor utilization\n- **Memory Usage** - RAM consumption\n- **Disk Usage** - Storage capacity\n- **Network Traffic** - Bandwidth utilization\n- **Service Status** - Application health\n\n### 4.2 Wazuh Integration\n\n#### Setup Steps\n\n1. **Configure Wazuh Endpoint**\n```bash\n# In .env file\nWAZUH_ENDPOINTS=https://wazuh:55000\nWAZUH_USERNAME=admin\nWAZUH_PASSWORD=your-password\n```\n\n2. **Enable Wazuh Alerts**\n```xml\n<!-- ossec.conf -->\n<integration>\n  <name>custom-webhook</name>\n  <hook_url>http://itechsmart:5000/webhook/wazuh</hook_url>\n  <level>7</level>\n  <alert_format>json</alert_format>\n</integration>\n```\n\n#### Monitored Events\n\n- **Authentication Failures** - Brute force detection\n- **File Integrity** - Unauthorized file changes\n- **Rootkit Detection** - Malware scanning\n- **Vulnerability Detection** - Security patches\n- **Log Analysis** - Suspicious patterns\n\n### 4.3 GitHub Integration\n\n#### Setup Steps\n\n1. **Create Webhook**\n   - Go to GitHub repository â†’ Settings â†’ Webhooks\n   - Add webhook URL: `http://your-server:5000/webhook/github`\n   - Select events: Workflow runs, Issues, Pull requests\n\n2. **Configure Secret**\n```bash\n# In .env file\nGITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET=your-secret-key\n```\n\n#### Monitored Events\n\n- **Workflow Failures** - CI/CD pipeline issues\n- **Deployment Failures** - Failed deployments\n- **Security Alerts** - Dependabot alerts\n- **Infrastructure Changes** - Terraform/IaC changes\n\n### 4.4 Custom Monitoring\n\n#### Add Custom Webhook\n\n```bash\n# Send custom alert\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/webhook/custom \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "severity": "high",\n    "host": "web-server-01",\n    "message": "Custom alert message",\n    "source": "custom-monitor"\n  }\'\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Alert Management\n\n### 5.1 Understanding Alerts\n\n#### Alert Lifecycle\n\n1. **Detection** - Issue detected by monitoring system\n2. **Reception** - Alert received by iTechSmart\n3. **Diagnosis** - AI analyzes root cause\n4. **Action Planning** - Remediation action proposed\n5. **Approval** - Manual approval (if required)\n6. **Execution** - Action executed\n7. **Verification** - Success verified\n8. **Notification** - Team notified\n9. **Logging** - Audit log created\n\n#### Alert Severity Levels\n\n**Critical** ðŸ”´\n- Immediate action required\n- Service outages\n- Security breaches\n- Data loss risk\n\n**High** ðŸŸ \n- Urgent attention needed\n- Performance degradation\n- Failed backups\n- Authentication issues\n\n**Medium** ðŸŸ¡\n- Should be addressed soon\n- Resource warnings\n- Configuration issues\n- Minor errors\n\n**Low** ðŸŸ¢\n- Informational\n- Routine events\n- Successful actions\n- Status updates\n\n### 5.2 Alert Actions\n\n#### View Alert Details\n\n1. Click on alert card in dashboard\n2. Review full alert information:\n   - Source system\n   - Affected host\n   - Diagnostic analysis\n   - Recommended actions\n   - Historical context\n\n#### Approve Action\n\n```bash\n# Via API\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/actions/{action_id}/approve \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN"\n\n# Via Dashboard\nClick "Approve" button on action card\n```\n\n#### Reject Action\n\n```bash\n# Via API\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/actions/{action_id}/reject \\\n  -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN" \\\n  -d \'{"reason": "Not appropriate at this time"}\'\n\n# Via Dashboard\nClick "Reject" button and provide reason\n```\n\n#### Manual Intervention\n\nIf automatic remediation isn\'t appropriate:\n\n1. Click "Manual Action" on alert\n2. Review diagnostic information\n3. Execute commands manually via SSH/RDP\n4. Mark alert as resolved\n5. Document actions taken\n\n### 5.3 Alert Filtering\n\n#### Filter by Severity\n\n```bash\n# Dashboard filter\nSelect severity: Critical, High, Medium, Low\n\n# API filter\nGET /api/alerts?severity=critical\n```\n\n#### Filter by Source\n\n```bash\n# Dashboard filter\nSelect source: Prometheus, Wazuh, GitHub\n\n# API filter\nGET /api/alerts?source=prometheus\n```\n\n#### Filter by Time\n\n```bash\n# Last 24 hours\nGET /api/alerts?since=24h\n\n# Last 7 days\nGET /api/alerts?since=7d\n\n# Custom range\nGET /api/alerts?start=2025-01-01&end=2025-01-31\n```\n\n### 5.4 Alert Notifications\n\nConfigure where alerts are sent:\n\n```bash\n# In .env file\nSLACK_WEBHOOK_URL=https://hooks.slack.com/...\nPAGERDUTY_API_KEY=your-key\nEMAIL_RECIPIENTS=admin@company.com,ops@company.com\n```\n\nSee [Section 8: Notification Setup](#8-notification-setup) for details.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Remediation Actions\n\n### 6.1 Action Types\n\n#### Command Execution\nExecute shell commands on remote systems:\n\n```python\n# SSH (Linux/Unix)\naction = {\n    "type": "ssh",\n    "host": "web-server-01",\n    "command": "systemctl restart nginx"\n}\n\n# WinRM (Windows)\naction = {\n    "type": "winrm",\n    "host": "win-server-01",\n    "command": "Restart-Service IIS"\n}\n\n# Telnet (Network Devices)\naction = {\n    "type": "telnet",\n    "host": "switch-01",\n    "command": "reload"\n}\n```\n\n#### Service Management\nRestart, stop, or start services:\n\n```bash\n# Restart service\nsystemctl restart nginx\n\n# Stop service\nsystemctl stop apache2\n\n# Start service\nsystemctl start postgresql\n```\n\n#### Process Management\nKill problematic processes:\n\n```bash\n# Kill by PID\nkill -9 12345\n\n# Kill by name\npkill -9 java\n\n# Kill all instances\nkillall -9 chrome\n```\n\n#### File Operations\nClean up disk space:\n\n```bash\n# Remove old logs\nfind /var/log -name "*.log" -mtime +30 -delete\n\n# Clean temp files\nrm -rf /tmp/*\n\n# Rotate logs\nlogrotate -f /etc/logrotate.conf\n```\n\n### 6.2 Action Safety\n\n#### Risk Levels\n\n**Low Risk** ðŸŸ¢\n- Read-only operations\n- Status checks\n- Log viewing\n- No approval required\n\n**Medium Risk** ðŸŸ¡\n- Service restarts\n- Log rotation\n- Configuration changes\n- Approval recommended\n\n**High Risk** ðŸ”´\n- Process termination\n- File deletion\n- Network changes\n- Approval required\n\n**Critical Risk** âš«\n- System reboots\n- Data deletion\n- Security changes\n- Multiple approvals required\n\n#### Safety Checks\n\niTechSmart validates all commands:\n\n```python\n# Dangerous patterns blocked\nDANGEROUS_PATTERNS = [\n    r\'rm\\s+-rf\\s+/\',      # Delete root\n    r\'dd\\s+if=\',          # Disk operations\n    r\'mkfs\\.\',            # Format disk\n    r\'shutdown\',          # System shutdown\n    r\'reboot\',            # System reboot\n]\n```\n\n### 6.3 Approval Workflows\n\n#### Automatic Approval\n\nFor low-risk actions:\n\n```bash\n# In .env file\nAUTO_REMEDIATION=true\nAUTO_APPROVE_LOW_RISK=true\n```\n\n#### Manual Approval\n\nFor high-risk actions:\n\n1. Action proposed\n2. Notification sent to approvers\n3. Approver reviews action\n4. Approver approves/rejects\n5. Action executed (if approved)\n\n#### Multi-Level Approval\n\nFor critical actions:\n\n```python\napproval_config = {\n    "required_approvals": 2,\n    "approvers": ["admin", "senior-ops"],\n    "timeout": 600  # 10 minutes\n}\n```\n\n### 6.4 Action Execution\n\n#### Execution Flow\n\n1. **Validation** - Command safety check\n2. **Credential Retrieval** - Get encrypted credentials\n3. **Connection** - Establish secure connection\n4. **Execution** - Run command\n5. **Output Capture** - Capture stdout/stderr\n6. **Verification** - Verify success\n7. **Logging** - Log to audit trail\n8. **Notification** - Notify team\n\n#### Execution Results\n\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "exit_code": 0,\n  "stdout": "Service restarted successfully",\n  "stderr": "",\n  "duration": 2.5,\n  "timestamp": "2025-01-15T10:30:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n### 6.5 Rollback Procedures\n\nIf action fails:\n\n1. **Automatic Rollback** - Restore previous state\n2. **Notification** - Alert team of failure\n3. **Manual Intervention** - Provide rollback instructions\n4. **Incident Creation** - Create incident ticket\n\n---\n\n## 7. Workflow Management\n\n### 7.1 Built-in Workflows\n\niTechSmart includes 5 pre-built workflows:\n\n#### Workflow #1: High CPU Remediation\n**Trigger:** CPU > 80%  \n**Steps:**\n1. Identify top CPU processes\n2. Notify team\n3. Wait for approval\n4. Kill process (if approved)\n5. Verify CPU normalized\n6. Log incident\n\n#### Workflow #2: Service Restart\n**Trigger:** Service down  \n**Steps:**\n1. Check service status\n2. Backup configuration\n3. Stop service\n4. Wait 5 seconds\n5. Start service\n6. Verify service running\n7. Notify success\n\n#### Workflow #3: Security Incident\n**Trigger:** Critical Wazuh alert  \n**Steps:**\n1. Isolate host\n2. Collect evidence\n3. Notify security team\n4. Create P1 ticket\n5. Wait for investigation\n\n#### Workflow #4: Disk Space Cleanup\n**Trigger:** Disk > 85%  \n**Steps:**\n1. Analyze disk usage\n2. Clean temp files\n3. Rotate logs\n4. Verify space freed\n5. Notify team\n\n#### Workflow #5: Database Optimization\n**Trigger:** Query time > 5s  \n**Steps:**\n1. Identify slow queries\n2. Check connection pool\n3. Analyze table statistics\n4. Notify DBA team\n5. Wait for approval\n6. Run VACUUM ANALYZE\n7. Verify performance\n8. Create report\n\n### 7.2 Creating Custom Workflows\n\n#### YAML Definition\n\n```yaml\nname: Custom Workflow\ndescription: My custom automation workflow\ntrigger:\n  type: alert\n  condition: metric_name > threshold\n\nsteps:\n  - name: Step 1\n    action_type: command\n    parameters:\n      command: "echo \'Starting workflow\'"\n    \n  - name: Step 2\n    action_type: notification\n    parameters:\n      channels: [\'slack\']\n      message: "Workflow started"\n    \n  - name: Step 3\n    action_type: approval\n    parameters:\n      timeout: 300\n      approvers: [\'admin\']\n```\n\n#### Python API\n\n```python\nfrom itechsmart_supreme.features.workflow_engine import WorkflowEngine\n\nengine = WorkflowEngine()\n\n# Create workflow\nworkflow = engine.create_workflow(\n    name="My Workflow",\n    description="Custom workflow",\n    trigger={"type": "alert"},\n    steps=[\n        {\n            "name": "Check Status",\n            "action_type": "command",\n            "parameters": {"command": "uptime"}\n        }\n    ]\n)\n\n# Execute workflow\nresult = await engine.execute_workflow(\n    workflow_id=workflow.id,\n    context={"host": "server-01"}\n)\n```\n\n### 7.3 Workflow Templates\n\nUse templates for common scenarios:\n\n```python\n# Create from template\nworkflow = engine.create_workflow_from_template(\n    template_name=\'high_cpu_remediation\',\n    parameters={\n        \'cpu_threshold\': 90,\n        \'approval_timeout\': 600\n    }\n)\n```\n\n### 7.4 Workflow Monitoring\n\nTrack workflow execution:\n\n```bash\n# List running workflows\nGET /api/workflows/running\n\n# Get workflow status\nGET /api/workflows/{workflow_id}/status\n\n# View workflow history\nGET /api/workflows/history\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. Notification Setup\n\n### 8.1 Supported Channels\n\niTechSmart supports 7 notification channels:\n\n1. **Slack** - Team collaboration\n2. **Email** - Documentation and audit\n3. **PagerDuty** - On-call escalation\n4. **Microsoft Teams** - Enterprise teams\n5. **Telegram** - Mobile notifications\n6. **SMS** - Emergency alerts\n7. **Webhooks** - Custom integrations\n\n### 8.2 Slack Configuration\n\n```bash\n# 1. Create Slack webhook\n# Go to: https://api.slack.com/messaging/webhooks\n\n# 2. Configure in .env\nSLACK_WEBHOOK_URL=https://hooks.slack.com/services/YOUR/WEBHOOK/URL\n\n# 3. Test notification\ncurl -X POST $SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL \\\n  -d \'{"text":"Test from iTechSmart"}\'\n```\n\n**Features:**\n- Rich message formatting\n- Thread support\n- Emoji indicators\n- Instant delivery\n\n### 8.3 Email Configuration\n\n```bash\n# Configure SMTP\nSMTP_SERVER=smtp.gmail.com\nSMTP_PORT=587\nSMTP_USERNAME=your-email@gmail.com\nSMTP_PASSWORD=your-app-password\nFROM_EMAIL=alerts@itechsmart.dev\nEMAIL_RECIPIENTS=admin@company.com,ops@company.com\n```\n\n**Gmail Setup:**\n1. Enable 2-factor authentication\n2. Generate app password\n3. Use app password in configuration\n\n### 8.4 PagerDuty Configuration\n\n```bash\n# 1. Create PagerDuty integration\n# Go to: Services â†’ Your Service â†’ Integrations\n\n# 2. Configure in .env\nPAGERDUTY_API_KEY=your-integration-key\nPAGERDUTY_SERVICE_ID=your-service-id\n\n# 3. Test incident\ncurl -X POST https://events.pagerduty.com/v2/enqueue \\\n  -d \'{\n    "routing_key": "YOUR_KEY",\n    "event_action": "trigger",\n    "payload": {\n      "summary": "Test from iTechSmart",\n      "severity": "error",\n      "source": "itechsmart"\n    }\n  }\'\n```\n\n### 8.5 Microsoft Teams Configuration\n\n```bash\n# 1. Create Teams webhook\n# Go to: Channel â†’ Connectors â†’ Incoming Webhook\n\n# 2. Configure in .env\nTEAMS_WEBHOOK_URL=https://outlook.office.com/webhook/YOUR/WEBHOOK/URL\n\n# 3. Test message\ncurl -X POST $TEAMS_WEBHOOK_URL \\\n  -d \'{\n    "@type": "MessageCard",\n    "title": "Test from iTechSmart",\n    "text": "This is a test message"\n  }\'\n```\n\n### 8.6 Telegram Configuration\n\n```bash\n# 1. Create Telegram bot\n# Talk to @BotFather on Telegram\n\n# 2. Get chat ID\n# Send message to bot, then:\ncurl https://api.telegram.org/bot<TOKEN>/getUpdates\n\n# 3. Configure in .env\nTELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN=your-bot-token\nTELEGRAM_CHAT_ID=your-chat-id\n```\n\n### 8.7 Notification Routing\n\nConfigure smart routing by severity:\n\n```python\nnotification_rules = {\n    "critical": ["pagerduty", "slack", "sms"],\n    "high": ["slack", "email", "teams"],\n    "medium": ["slack", "email"],\n    "low": ["email"]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 9. Security & Credentials\n\n### 9.1 Credential Management\n\n#### Adding Credentials\n\n```bash\n# Via API\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/credentials \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "host": "web-server-01",\n    "username": "admin",\n    "password": "secure-password",\n    "protocol": "ssh"\n  }\'\n\n# Via Dashboard\n1. Go to Settings â†’ Credentials\n2. Click "Add Credential"\n3. Fill in details\n4. Click "Save"\n```\n\n#### Credential Storage\n\nAll credentials are:\n- **Encrypted** using Fernet encryption\n- **Salted** with PBKDF2 key derivation\n- **Protected** by master password\n- **Stored** in encrypted database\n\n#### Credential Retrieval\n\n```python\nfrom itechsmart_supreme.security.credential_manager import CredentialManager\n\nmanager = CredentialManager(master_password)\n\n# Get credentials\ncreds = manager.get_credentials(\n    host="web-server-01",\n    protocol="ssh"\n)\n```\n\n### 9.2 Authentication\n\n#### API Authentication\n\n```bash\n# Get token\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/auth/login \\\n  -d \'{"username":"admin","password":"password"}\'\n\n# Use token\ncurl -H "Authorization: Bearer YOUR_TOKEN" \\\n  http://localhost:5000/api/alerts\n```\n\n#### Session Management\n\n- **Session Timeout:** 30 minutes\n- **Token Expiry:** 24 hours\n- **Refresh Tokens:** Supported\n- **Multi-Factor:** Optional\n\n### 9.3 Zero Trust Security\n\niTechSmart implements zero trust principles:\n\n**Never Trust, Always Verify:**\n- Continuous authentication\n- Risk-based access control\n- Least privilege access\n- Complete audit logging\n\n**Trust Levels:**\n- **VERIFIED** - Full access\n- **HIGH** - Most operations\n- **MEDIUM** - Limited operations\n- **LOW** - Read-only\n- **UNTRUSTED** - No access\n\n### 9.4 Audit Logging\n\nAll actions are logged:\n\n```json\n{\n  "timestamp": "2025-01-15T10:30:00Z",\n  "user": "admin",\n  "action": "execute_command",\n  "host": "web-server-01",\n  "command": "systemctl restart nginx",\n  "result": "success",\n  "ip_address": "192.168.1.100"\n}\n```\n\nView audit logs:\n\n```bash\n# Via API\nGET /api/audit/logs\n\n# Via Dashboard\nNavigate to Logs â†’ Audit Trail\n```\n\n### 9.5 Kill Switch\n\nEmergency stop for all automation:\n\n```bash\n# Enable kill switch\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/killswitch/enable\n\n# Disable kill switch\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/killswitch/disable\n\n# Check status\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/killswitch/status\n```\n\nWhen enabled:\n- âŒ No automatic actions\n- âŒ No command execution\n- âœ… Monitoring continues\n- âœ… Alerts still received\n- âœ… Manual actions allowed\n\n---\n\n## 10. API Usage\n\n### 10.1 API Overview\n\niTechSmart provides a RESTful API for all operations.\n\n**Base URL:** `http://localhost:5000/api`\n\n**Authentication:** Bearer token\n\n**Content-Type:** `application/json`\n\n### 10.2 Core Endpoints\n\n#### Health Check\n\n```bash\nGET /api/health\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "status": "healthy",\n  "version": "1.0.0",\n  "uptime": 3600\n}\n```\n\n#### System Status\n\n```bash\nGET /api/status\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "monitoring": {\n    "prometheus": "connected",\n    "wazuh": "connected"\n  },\n  "active_alerts": 5,\n  "pending_actions": 2,\n  "kill_switch": false\n}\n```\n\n### 10.3 Alert Endpoints\n\n#### List Alerts\n\n```bash\nGET /api/alerts?severity=critical&limit=10\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "alerts": [\n    {\n      "id": "alert-123",\n      "severity": "critical",\n      "host": "web-server-01",\n      "message": "High CPU usage",\n      "timestamp": "2025-01-15T10:30:00Z"\n    }\n  ],\n  "total": 5,\n  "page": 1\n}\n```\n\n#### Get Alert Details\n\n```bash\nGET /api/alerts/{alert_id}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "id": "alert-123",\n  "severity": "critical",\n  "host": "web-server-01",\n  "message": "High CPU usage",\n  "diagnosis": {\n    "root_cause": "Runaway process",\n    "confidence": 0.95\n  },\n  "recommended_actions": [...]\n}\n```\n\n### 10.4 Action Endpoints\n\n#### List Actions\n\n```bash\nGET /api/actions?status=pending\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "actions": [\n    {\n      "id": "action-456",\n      "description": "Kill process 12345",\n      "risk_level": "high",\n      "status": "pending_approval"\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Approve Action\n\n```bash\nPOST /api/actions/{action_id}/approve\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "action_id": "action-456",\n  "status": "approved",\n  "execution_scheduled": true\n}\n```\n\n#### Reject Action\n\n```bash\nPOST /api/actions/{action_id}/reject\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "reason": "Not appropriate at this time"\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "action_id": "action-456",\n  "status": "rejected"\n}\n```\n\n### 10.5 Workflow Endpoints\n\n#### List Workflows\n\n```bash\nGET /api/workflows\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "workflows": [\n    {\n      "id": "workflow-789",\n      "name": "High CPU Remediation",\n      "status": "running",\n      "current_step": 3\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Execute Workflow\n\n```bash\nPOST /api/workflows/{workflow_id}/execute\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "context": {\n    "host": "web-server-01"\n  }\n}\n\nResponse:\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "workflow_id": "workflow-789",\n  "execution_id": "exec-123"\n}\n```\n\n### 10.6 Webhook Endpoints\n\n#### Prometheus Webhook\n\n```bash\nPOST /webhook/prometheus\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "alerts": [\n    {\n      "status": "firing",\n      "labels": {\n        "alertname": "HighCPU",\n        "instance": "web-server-01"\n      },\n      "annotations": {\n        "summary": "High CPU usage detected"\n      }\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n#### Wazuh Webhook\n\n```bash\nPOST /webhook/wazuh\nContent-Type: application/json\n\n{\n  "rule": {\n    "level": 10,\n    "description": "Authentication failure"\n  },\n  "agent": {\n    "name": "web-server-01"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Troubleshooting\n\n### 11.1 Common Issues\n\n#### Dashboard Not Loading\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Blank page\n- Connection refused\n- 502 Bad Gateway\n\n**Solutions:**\n```bash\n# Check if service is running\ndocker-compose ps\n\n# Check logs\ndocker-compose logs -f itechsmart-supreme\n\n# Restart service\ndocker-compose restart itechsmart-supreme\n\n# Check port availability\nnetstat -tulpn | grep 5000\n```\n\n#### Alerts Not Appearing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- No alerts in dashboard\n- Monitoring connected but no data\n\n**Solutions:**\n```bash\n# Verify monitoring endpoints\ncurl http://prometheus:9090/api/v1/query?query=up\n\n# Check webhook configuration\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/webhook/test\n\n# Review logs\ntail -f itechsmart_supreme.log | grep "alert"\n\n# Test alert manually\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/webhook/custom \\\n  -d \'{"severity":"high","message":"Test alert"}\'\n```\n\n#### Actions Not Executing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Actions stuck in pending\n- Execution failures\n- Timeout errors\n\n**Solutions:**\n```bash\n# Check credentials\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/credentials/test\n\n# Verify SSH connectivity\nssh user@target-host\n\n# Check action logs\nGET /api/actions/{action_id}/logs\n\n# Review execution history\nGET /api/actions/history?status=failed\n```\n\n#### Notifications Not Sending\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- No Slack messages\n- Emails not received\n- PagerDuty not triggered\n\n**Solutions:**\n```bash\n# Test Slack webhook\ncurl -X POST $SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL \\\n  -d \'{"text":"Test"}\'\n\n# Test email configuration\npython -c "from itechsmart_supreme.features.notification_manager import NotificationManager; NotificationManager(config).test_email()"\n\n# Check notification logs\ngrep "notification" itechsmart_supreme.log\n\n# Verify channel configuration\nGET /api/notifications/channels\n```\n\n### 11.2 Performance Issues\n\n#### High CPU Usage\n\n```bash\n# Check process usage\ntop -p $(pgrep -f itechsmart)\n\n# Review monitoring frequency\n# Reduce polling intervals in .env\nPROMETHEUS_POLL_INTERVAL=60\nWAZUH_POLL_INTERVAL=60\n```\n\n#### High Memory Usage\n\n```bash\n# Check memory usage\ndocker stats itechsmart-supreme\n\n# Clear cache\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/cache/clear\n\n# Adjust memory limits\n# In docker-compose.yml\nmem_limit: 2g\n```\n\n#### Slow Response Times\n\n```bash\n# Enable debug mode\nexport FLASK_DEBUG=1\n\n# Check database performance\nsqlite3 itechsmart.db "ANALYZE;"\n\n# Review slow queries\nGET /api/debug/slow-queries\n```\n\n### 11.3 Connection Issues\n\n#### SSH Connection Failures\n\n```bash\n# Test SSH manually\nssh -v user@host\n\n# Check SSH key permissions\nchmod 600 ~/.ssh/id_rsa\n\n# Verify known_hosts\nssh-keyscan host >> ~/.ssh/known_hosts\n\n# Check firewall rules\nsudo iptables -L | grep 22\n```\n\n#### WinRM Connection Failures\n\n```bash\n# Test WinRM\nwinrs -r:http://host:5985 -u:user -p:pass ipconfig\n\n# Enable WinRM on Windows\nEnable-PSRemoting -Force\n\n# Check WinRM configuration\nwinrm get winrm/config\n```\n\n### 11.4 Debug Mode\n\nEnable detailed logging:\n\n```bash\n# Set environment variable\nexport Best Practices\n\n### 12.1 Security Best Practices\n\n1. **Use Strong Master Password**\n   - Minimum 16 characters\n   - Mix of letters, numbers, symbols\n   - Store securely (password manager)\n\n2. **Enable Multi-Factor Authentication**\n   ```bash\n   MFA_ENABLED=true\n   MFA_METHOD=totp\n   ```\n\n3. **Rotate Credentials Regularly**\n   - Change passwords every 90 days\n   - Update API keys quarterly\n   - Review access logs monthly\n\n4. **Limit Auto-Remediation**\n   ```bash\n   AUTO_REMEDIATION=false\n   AUTO_APPROVE_LOW_RISK=true\n   AUTO_APPROVE_HIGH_RISK=false\n   ```\n\n5. **Enable Audit Logging**\n   ```bash\n   AUDIT_LOGGING=true\n   AUDIT_LOG_RETENTION=365\n   ```\n\n### 12.2 Operational Best Practices\n\n1. **Start with Monitoring Only**\n   - Disable auto-remediation initially\n   - Observe alerts for 1-2 weeks\n   - Gradually enable automation\n\n2. **Test in Non-Production First**\n   - Deploy to dev/staging environment\n   - Run demo scenarios\n   - Verify all integrations\n\n3. **Configure Approval Workflows**\n   - Require approval for high-risk actions\n   - Set appropriate timeouts\n   - Define clear approver roles\n\n4. **Set Up Notifications**\n   - Configure multiple channels\n   - Test all notification methods\n   - Set up escalation policies\n\n5. **Regular Maintenance**\n   - Review audit logs weekly\n   - Update credentials monthly\n   - Check system health daily\n\n### 12.3 Performance Best Practices\n\n1. **Optimize Polling Intervals**\n   ```bash\n   PROMETHEUS_POLL_INTERVAL=60  # 1 minute\n   WAZUH_POLL_INTERVAL=60       # 1 minute\n   ```\n\n2. **Limit Alert History**\n   ```bash\n   ALERT_RETENTION_DAYS=30\n   ACTION_RETENTION_DAYS=90\n   ```\n\n3. **Use Database Indexing**\n   ```sql\n   CREATE INDEX idx_alerts_timestamp ON alerts(timestamp);\n   CREATE INDEX idx_actions_status ON actions(status);\n   ```\n\n4. **Enable Caching**\n   ```bash\n   CACHE_ENABLED=true\n   CACHE_TTL=300  # 5 minutes\n   ```\n\n### 12.4 Monitoring Best Practices\n\n1. **Monitor iTechSmart Itself**\n   - Set up health checks\n   - Monitor resource usage\n   - Alert on failures\n\n2. **Regular Testing**\n   - Test workflows monthly\n   - Verify integrations weekly\n   - Run demo scenarios quarterly\n\n3. **Documentation**\n   - Document custom workflows\n   - Maintain runbooks\n   - Update procedures regularly\n\n---\n\n## 13. Advanced Features\n\n### 13.1 Multi-AI Provider Support\n\niTechSmart supports multiple AI providers:\n\n```bash\n# Configure AI providers\nAI_PROVIDERS=openai,gemini,claude,ollama\nAI_FALLBACK_CHAIN=openai,gemini,claude,ollama\n\n# OpenAI\nOPENAI_API_KEY=your-key\nOPENAI_MODEL=gpt-4\n\n# Google Gemini\nGEMINI_API_KEY=your-key\nGEMINI_MODEL=gemini-pro\n\n# Anthropic Claude\nANTHROPIC_API_KEY=your-key\nANTHROPIC_MODEL=claude-3-opus\n\n# Ollama (local)\nOLLAMA_BASE_URL=http://localhost:11434\nOLLAMA_MODEL=llama2\n```\n\n### 13.2 Custom Integrations\n\n#### Create Custom Monitor\n\n```python\nfrom itechsmart_supreme.monitoring.base_monitor import BaseMonitor\n\nclass CustomMonitor(BaseMonitor):\n    def __init__(self, config):\n        super().__init__(config)\n        \n    async def collect_metrics(self):\n        # Your custom logic\n        metrics = await self.fetch_data()\n        return self.process_metrics(metrics)\n```\n\n#### Create Custom Action\n\n```python\nfrom itechsmart_supreme.execution.base_executor import BaseExecutor\n\nclass CustomExecutor(BaseExecutor):\n    async def execute(self, action):\n        # Your custom execution logic\n        result = await self.run_custom_action(action)\n        return result\n```\n\n### 13.3 Integration with External Tools\n\n#### Ansible Integration\n\n```python\nfrom itechsmart_supreme.integrations.ansible_integration import AnsibleIntegration\n\nansible = AnsibleIntegration(config)\n\n# Run playbook\nresult = await ansible.run_playbook(\n    playbook_path="site.yml",\n    inventory="hosts",\n    extra_vars={"target": "web-servers"}\n)\n```\n\n#### SaltStack Integration\n\n```python\nfrom itechsmart_supreme.integrations.saltstack_integration import SaltStackIntegration\n\nsalt = SaltStackIntegration(config)\n\n# Execute state\nresult = await salt.execute_state(\n    target="web-*",\n    state="nginx.restart"\n)\n```\n\n### 13.4 Advanced Workflows\n\n#### Conditional Branching\n\n```yaml\nsteps:\n  - name: Check Condition\n    action_type: check\n    parameters:\n      metric: cpu_usage\n      condition: "> 80"\n    on_success: High CPU Path\n    on_failure: Normal Path\n    \n  - name: High CPU Path\n    action_type: command\n    parameters:\n      command: "kill -9 {pid}"\n      \n  - name: Normal Path\n    action_type: notification\n    parameters:\n      message: "CPU normal"\n```\n\n#### Parallel Execution\n\n```yaml\nsteps:\n  - name: Parallel Tasks\n    action_type: parallel\n    tasks:\n      - name: Task 1\n        action_type: command\n        parameters:\n          command: "task1.sh"\n      - name: Task 2\n        action_type: command\n        parameters:\n          command: "task2.sh"\n```\n\n### 13.5 Custom Dashboards\n\nCreate custom Grafana dashboards:\n\n```json\n{\n  "dashboard": {\n    "title": "iTechSmart Metrics",\n    "panels": [\n      {\n        "title": "Alert Rate",\n        "targets": [\n          {\n            "expr": "rate(itechsmart_alerts_total[5m])"\n          }\n        ]\n      }\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 14. FAQ\n\n### 14.1 General Questions\n\n**Q: What is iTechSmart Supreme?**  \nA: An autonomous IT infrastructure healing platform that detects, diagnoses, and resolves issues automatically.\n\n**Q: Is it safe to use in production?**  \nA: Yes, with proper configuration. Start with monitoring only, then gradually enable automation with approval workflows.\n\n**Q: What systems does it support?**  \nA: Linux, Windows, network devices, cloud platforms, and any system with SSH/WinRM/Telnet access.\n\n**Q: Does it require internet access?**  \nA: No, it can run in offline mode using the built-in rule-based diagnosis engine.\n\n### 14.2 Technical Questions\n\n**Q: How does AI diagnosis work?**  \nA: It uses multiple AI providers (OpenAI, Gemini, Claude, Ollama) with automatic fallback, or offline rule-based analysis.\n\n**Q: Can I customize workflows?**  \nA: Yes, you can create custom workflows using YAML or Python API.\n\n**Q: How are credentials stored?**  \nA: All credentials are encrypted using Fernet encryption with PBKDF2 key derivation.\n\n**Q: What happens if iTechSmart fails?**  \nA: Monitoring systems continue to operate independently. iTechSmart is designed for high availability with automatic recovery.\n\n### 14.3 Operational Questions\n\n**Q: How long does remediation take?**  \nA: Typically 10-30 seconds from detection to resolution, depending on action complexity.\n\n**Q: Can I rollback actions?**  \nA: Yes, failed actions trigger automatic rollback procedures.\n\n**Q: How do I handle false positives?**  \nA: Use approval workflows, adjust alert thresholds, and create custom filters.\n\n**Q: What\'s the learning curve?**  \nA: Basic usage: 1 day. Advanced features: 1 week. Full mastery: 1 month.\n\n### 14.4 Pricing & Licensing\n\n**Q: What\'s the license?**  \nA: MIT License - free for commercial and personal use.\n\n**Q: Are there any costs?**  \nA: Only if using external AI providers (OpenAI, etc.). Offline mode is completely free.\n\n**Q: Can I modify the code?**  \nA: Yes, it\'s open source under MIT license.\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“š Additional Resources\n\n### Documentation\n- **README.md** - Complete feature documentation\n- **DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE.md** - Production deployment guide\n- **DEMO_SCENARIOS.md** - Interactive demo scenarios\n- **INTEGRATIONS_GUIDE.md** - Tool integration guide\n- **ENHANCED_FEATURES.md** - Advanced features guide\n- **WORKFLOW_TEMPLATES_AND_NOTIFICATIONS.md** - Workflow and notification guide\n\n### Quick References\n- **QUICK_START.md** - 5-minute quick start\n- **QUICK_REFERENCE_WORKFLOWS_NOTIFICATIONS.md** - Workflow quick reference\n- **INDEX.md** - Documentation index\n\n### Configuration\n- **.env.example** - Environment configuration template\n- **docker-compose.yml** - Docker deployment\n- **prometheus.yml** - Prometheus configuration\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“ž Support & Contact\n\n### Getting Help\n1. **Documentation** - Check this manual and other guides\n2. **Logs** - Review application and system logs\n3. **GitHub Issues** - Report bugs and request features\n4. **Community** - Join user discussions\n\n### Reporting Issues\nWhen reporting issues, include:\n- iTechSmart version\n- Operating system\n- Error messages\n- Steps to reproduce\n- Relevant logs\n\n---\n\n**iTechSmart Supreme User Manual v1.0.0**  \n**Last Updated: January 2025**  \n**Â© 2025 NinjaTech AI. SPDX-License-Identifier: MIT\npragma solidity ^0.8.20;\n\nimport "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/ERC20.sol";\nimport "@openzeppelin/contracts/token/ERC20/extensions/ERC20Burnable.sol";\nimport "@openzeppelin/contracts/access/Ownable.sol";\nimport "@openzeppelin/contracts/security/Pausable.sol";\n\ncontract iTechSmartToken is ERC20, ERC20Burnable, Ownable, Pausable {\n    uint256 public constant MAX_SUPPLY = 100000 * 10**18; // 100,000 tokens\n    \n    // Vesting schedules\n    mapping(address => VestingSchedule) public vestingSchedules;\n    \n    struct VestingSchedule {\n        uint256 totalAmount;\n        uint256 releasedAmount;\n        uint256 startTime;\n        uint256 duration;\n    }\n    \n    constructor() ERC20("iTechSmart Token", "ITECH") {\n        // Mint initial supply to contract owner\n        _mint(msg.sender, MAX_SUPPLY);\n    }\n    \n    // Pause token transfers in emergency\n    function pause() public onlyOwner {\n        _pause();\n    }\n    \n    function unpause() public onlyOwner {\n        _unpause();\n    }\n    \n    // Override transfer to add pause functionality\n    function _beforeTokenTransfer(\n        address from,\n        address to,\n        uint256 amount\n    ) internal override whenNotPaused {\n        super._beforeTokenTransfer(from, to, amount);\n    }\n    \n    // Vesting function for team tokens\n    function createVestingSchedule(\n        address beneficiary,\n        uint256 amount,\n        uint256 duration\n    ) public onlyOwner {\n        require(vestingSchedules[beneficiary].totalAmount == 0, "Schedule exists");\n        \n        vestingSchedules[beneficiary] = VestingSchedule({\n            totalAmount: amount,\n            releasedAmount: 0,\n            startTime: block.timestamp,\n            duration: duration\n        });\n        \n        transfer(address(this), amount);\n    }\n    \n    // Release vested tokens\n    function releaseVestedTokens() public {\n        VestingSchedule storage schedule = vestingSchedules[msg.sender];\n        require(schedule.totalAmount > 0, "No vesting schedule");\n        \n        uint256 elapsed = block.timestamp - schedule.startTime;\n        uint256 vested = (schedule.totalAmount * elapsed) / schedule.duration;\n        \n        if (vested > schedule.totalAmount) {\n            vested = schedule.totalAmount;\n        }\n        \n        uint256 releasable = vested - schedule.releasedAmount;\n        require(releasable > 0, "No tokens to release");\n        \n        schedule.releasedAmount += releasable;\n        _transfer(address(this), msg.sender, releasable);\n    }\n    \n    // Staking functionality\n    mapping(address => StakeInfo) public stakes;\n    \n    struct StakeInfo {\n        uint256 amount;\n        uint256 startTime;\n        uint256 rewardRate; // Annual percentage rate\n    }\n    \n    function stake(uint256 amount) public {\n        require(amount > 0, "Cannot stake 0");\n        require(balanceOf(msg.sender) >= amount, "Insufficient balance");\n        \n        // Transfer tokens to contract\n        _transfer(msg.sender, address(this), amount);\n        \n        stakes[msg.sender] = StakeInfo({\n            amount: amount,\n            startTime: block.timestamp,\n            rewardRate: 10 // 10% APR\n        });\n    }\n    \n    function unstake() public {\n        StakeInfo memory stakeInfo = stakes[msg.sender];\n        require(stakeInfo.amount > 0, "No stake found");\n        \n        // Calculate rewards\n        uint256 duration = block.timestamp - stakeInfo.startTime;\n        uint256 reward = (stakeInfo.amount * stakeInfo.rewardRate * duration) / (365 days * 100);\n        \n        // Transfer staked amount + rewards\n        _transfer(address(this), msg.sender, stakeInfo.amount + reward);\n        \n        delete stakes[msg.sender];\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Cost:** Free (using OpenZeppelin templates)\n\n#### Step 5: Test Smart Contract\n\nUse Hardhat or Truffle for testing:\n\n```bash\n# Install Hardhat\nnpm install --save-dev hardhat\n\n# Create test file\nnpx hardhat test\n\n# Run tests\nnpx hardhat test test/iTechSmartToken.test.js\n```\n\n**Cost:** Free\n\n#### Step 6: Security Audit\n\n**Budget Option ($200-300):**\n- Use automated tools: Slither, Mythril\n- Community audit iTechSmart\n\n**Add Web3 Dependencies:**\n\n```bash\ncd itechsmart_supreme\nnpm install web3 ethers @metamask/detect-provider\n```\n\n**Create Web3 Module:**\n\n```python\n# itechsmart_supreme/web3/token_integration.py\n\nfrom web3 import Web3\nfrom eth_account import Account\nimport json\n\nclass iTechSmartTokenIntegration:\n    def __init__(self, contract_address, abi_path, rpc_url):\n        self.w3 = Web3(Web3.HTTPProvider(rpc_url))\n        self.contract_address = contract_address\n        \n        # Load contract ABI\n        with open(abi_path, \'r\') as f:\n            self.contract_abi = json.load(f)\n        \n        self.contract = self.w3.eth.contract(\n            address=contract_address,\n            abi=self.contract_abi\n        )\n    \n    def check_token_balance(self, wallet_address):\n        """Check ITECH token balance"""\n        balance = self.contract.functions.balanceOf(wallet_address).call()\n        return self.w3.from_wei(balance, \'ether\')\n    \n    def verify_premium_access(self, wallet_address, required_tokens=10):\n        """Verify user has enough tokens for premium features"""\n        balance = self.check_token_balance(wallet_address)\n        return balance >= required_tokens\n    \n    def stake_tokens(self, wallet_address, private_key, amount):\n        """Stake tokens for benefits"""\n        nonce = self.w3.eth.get_transaction_count(wallet_address)\n        \n        # Build transaction\n        txn = self.contract.functions.stake(\n            self.w3.to_wei(amount, \'ether\')\n        ).build_transaction({\n            \'from\': wallet_address,\n            \'nonce\': nonce,\n            \'gas\': 200000,\n            \'gasPrice\': self.w3.eth.gas_price\n        })\n        \n        # Sign transaction\n        signed_txn = self.w3.eth.account.sign_transaction(txn, private_key)\n        \n        # Send transaction\n        tx_hash = self.w3.eth.send_raw_transaction(signed_txn.rawTransaction)\n        \n        return tx_hash.hex()\n    \n    def reward_user(self, user_wallet, amount, admin_private_key):\n        """Reward user with tokens"""\n        admin_account = Account.from_key(admin_private_key)\n        \n        nonce = self.w3.eth.get_transaction_count(admin_account.address)\n        \n        txn = self.contract.functions.transfer(\n            user_wallet,\n            self.w3.to_wei(amount, \'ether\')\n        ).build_transaction({\n            \'from\': admin_account.address,\n            \'nonce\': nonce,\n            \'gas\': 100000,\n            \'gasPrice\': self.w3.eth.gas_price\n        })\n        \n        signed_txn = self.w3.eth.account.sign_transaction(txn, admin_private_key)\n        tx_hash = self.w3.eth.send_raw_transaction(signed_txn.rawTransaction)\n        \n        return tx_hash.hex()\n```\n\n**Add Web3 Features to Dashboard:**\n\n```javascript\n// itechsmart_supreme/web/static/js/web3.js\n\nlet web3;\nlet userAccount;\nlet tokenContract;\n\nconst CONTRACT_ADDRESS = \'0x...\'; // Your deployed contract\nconst CONTRACT_ABI = [...]; // Your contract ABI\n\nasync function connectWallet() {\n    if (typeof window.ethereum !== \'undefined\') {\n        try {\n            // Request account access\n            const accounts = await window.ethereum.request({ \n                method: \'eth_requestAccounts\' \n            });\n            \n            userAccount = accounts[0];\n            web3 = new          document.getElementById(\'wallet-address\').textContent = \n                userAccount.substring(0, 6) + \'...\' + userAccount.substring(38);\n            \n            // Check token balance\n            await updateTokenBalance();\n            \n            // Check premium access\n            await checkPremiumAccess();\n            \n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\'Error connecting wallet:\', error);\n        }\n    } else {\n        alert(\'Please install MetaMask!\');\n    }\n}\n\nasync function updateTokenBalance() {\n    const balance = await parseFloat(balanceInEther).toFixed(2) + \' ITECH\';\n}\n\nasync function checkPremiumAccess() {\n    const balance = await tokenContract.methods.balanceOf(userAccount).call();\n    const balanceInEther = parseFloat(web3.utils.fromWei(balance, \'ether\'));\n    \n    if (balanceInEther >= 10) {\n        // Enable premium features\n        document.getElementById(\'premium-badge\').style.display = \'block\';\n        enablePremiumFeatures();\n    }\n}\n\nasync function stakeTokens(amount) {\n    try {\n        const amountInWei = web3.utils.toWei(amount.toString(), \'ether\');\n        \n        await tokenContract.methods.stake(amountInWei).send({\n            from: userAccount\n        });\n        \n        alert(\'Tokens staked successfully!\');\n        await updateTokenBalance();\n        \n    } catch (error) {\n        console.error(\'Error staking tokens:\', error);\n    }\n}\n\nfunction enablePremiumFeatures() {\n    // Unlock AI diagnosis with multiple providers\n    document.getElementById(\'multi-ai-toggle\').disabled = false;\n    \n    // Unlock advanced workflows\n    document.getElementById(\'advanced-workflows\').style.display = \'block\';\n    \n    // Unlock priority support\n    document.getElementById(\'priority-support\').style.display = \'block\';\n}\n```\n\n**Add to Dashboard HTML:**\n\n```html\n<!-- itechsmart_supreme/web/templates/dashboard.html -->\n\n<div class="web3-section">\n    <button onclick="connectWallet()" Token-Gated Features\n\n**Premium Tier (10 ITECH):**\n- Multi-AI provider access\n- Advanced workflow templates\n- Priority support\n- Custom integrations\n\n**Enterprise Tier (100 ITECH):**\n- Unlimited AI queries\n- White-label solution\n- Dedicated support\n- Custom development\n\n**Implementation:**\n```python\ndef check_access_tier(wallet_address):\n    balance = token_integration.check_token_balance(wallet_address)\n    \n    if balance >= 100:\n        return "enterprise"\n    elif balance >= 10:\n        return "premium"\n    else:\n        return "basic"\n```\n\n### 2. Governance\n\n**Token Holders Can Vote On:**\n- New feature development\n- Workflow template additions\n- Integration priorities\n- Platform upgrades\n\n**Implementation:**\n```solidity\ncontract iTechSmartGovernance {\n    struct Proposal {\n        string description;\n        uint256 votesFor;\n        uint256 votesAgainst;\n        uint256 deadline;\n        bool executed;\n    }\n    \n    mapping(uint256 => Proposal) public proposals;\n    mapping(uint256 => mapping(address => bool)) public hasVoted;\n    \n    function createProposal(string memory description) public {\n        // Only token holders can create proposals\n        require(token.balanceOf(msg.sender) >= 100, "Need 100 tokens");\n        // Create proposal logic\n    }\n    \n    function vote(uint256 proposalId, bool support) public {\n        require(!hasVoted[proposalId][msg.sender], "Already voted");\n        \n        uint256 votes = token.balanceOf(msg.sender);\n        \n        if (support) {\n            proposals[proposalId].votesFor += votes;\n        } else {\n            proposals[proposalId].votesAgainst += votes;\n        }\n        \n        hasVoted[proposalId][msg.sender] = true;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Rewards & Incentives\n\n**Earn Tokens For:**\n- Reporting bugs: 10-100 ITECH\n- Creating workflows: 50 ITECH\n- Writing documentation: 25 ITECH\n- Referrals: 5 ITECH per user\n- Community support: 1-10 ITECH\n\n**Implementation:**\n```python\ndef reward_contribution(user_wallet, contribution_type):\n    rewards = {\n        \'bug_report\': 10,\n        \'workflow\': 50,\n        \'documentation\': 25,\n        \'referral\': 5,\n        \'support\': 5\n    }\n    \n    amount = rewards.get(contribution_type, 0)\n    \n    if amount > 0:\n        tx_hash = token_integration.reward_user(\n            user_wallet,\n            amount,\n            admin_private_key\n        )\n        \n        return tx_hash\n```\n\n### 4. Staking Benefits\n\n**Stake Tokens to Get:**\n- Reduced platform fees (10% off per 100 staked)\n- Early access to features\n- Exclusive workflow templates\n- Voting power multiplier\n- Revenue sharing (10% APR)\n\n**Implementation:**\n```python\ndef calculate_fee_discount(wallet_address):\n    stake_info = token_integration.get_stake_info(wallet_address)\n    staked_amount = stake_info[\'amount\']\n    \n    # 10% discount per 100 tokens staked, max 50%\n    discount = min(0.5, (staked_amount / 100) * 0.1)\n    \n    return discount\n```\n\n### 5. NFT Integration\n\n**Create NFTs For:**\n- Workflow templates (tradeable)\n- Achievement badges\n- Premium access passes\n- Limited edition features\n\n**Implementation:**\n```solidity\ncontract iTechSmartNFT is ERC721 {\n    struct WorkflowNFT {\n        string name;\n        string workflowData;\n        address creator;\n        uint256 royalty;\n    }\n    \n    mapping(uint256 => WorkflowNFT) public workflows;\n    \n    function mintWorkflow(\n        string memory name,\n        string memory workflowData\n    ) public {\n        require(token.balanceOf(msg.sender) >= 10, "Need 10 tokens");\n        \n        uint256 tokenId = totalSupply() + 1;\n        _mint(msg.sender, tokenId);\n        \n        workflows[tokenId] = WorkflowNFT({\n            name: name,\n            workflowData: workflowData,\n            creator: msg.sender,\n            royalty: 10 // 10% royalty to creator\n        });\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 6. DAO Structure\n\n**Create iTechSmart DAO:**\n- Community-governed platform\n- Treasury management\n- Development priorities\n- Partnership decisions\n\n**Implementation:**\n```solidity\ncontract iTechSmartDAO {\n    address public token;\n    address public treasury;\n    \n    struct Proposal {\n        string title;\n        string description;\n        uint256 amount;\n        address recipient;\n        uint256 votesFor;\n        uint256 votesAgainst;\n        bool executed;\n    }\n    \n    function executeProposal(uint256 proposalId) public {\n        Proposal storage proposal = proposals[proposalId];\n        \n        require(!proposal.executed, "Already executed");\n        require(\n            proposal.votesFor > proposal.votesAgainst,\n            "Proposal rejected"\n        );\n        \n        // Execute proposal\n        payable(proposal.recipient).transfer(proposal.amount);\n        proposal.executed = true;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## ðŸ“Š Financial Projections\n\n### Initial Investment: $1,000\n\n**Breakdown:**\n- Smart Contract: $200\n- Security Audit: $250\n- Deployment: $50\n- Initial Liquidity: $400\n- Marketing: $100\n\n### Revenue Projections (Year 1)\n\n**Scenario 1: Conservative**\n- Token Price: $1.00\n- Market Cap: $100,000\n- Monthly Revenue: $2,000\n- ROI: 24x\n\n**Scenario 2: Moderate**\n- Token Price: $5.00\n- Market Cap: $500,000\n- Monthly Revenue: $10,000\n- ROI: 120x\n\n**Scenario 3: Optimistic**\n- Token Price: $20.00\n- Market Cap: $2,000,000\n- Monthly Revenue: $50,000\n- ROI: 600x\n\n### Revenue Streams\n\n1. **Token Sales:** $15,000 (initial sale)\n2. **Platform Fees:** $1,000/month\n3. **Premium Subscriptions:** $2,000/month\n4. **Enterprise Licenses:** $5,000/month\n5. **Staking Fees:** $500/month\n6. **NFT Marketplace:** $1,000/month\n\n**Total Monthly Revenue:** $9,500\n\n---\n\n## âš–ï¸ Legal & Regulatory Considerations\n\n### Important Disclaimers\n\n**âš ï¸ WARNING: This is NOT legal advice. Scale resources\n\n```bash\n# Check resource usage\ndocker stats\n\n# Check database\ndocker-compose exec postgres psql -U postgres -c "SELECT * FROM pg_stat_activity;"\n\n# Check
